Upon approaching Carsons, you realize that sidewalks lead to both the front and back entrances of the building.\n\nYou enter through\n[[Carsons Front Door|Enter Carsons]]\n[[Carsons Back Door|Enter Carsons]]
[img[bing-wiscmap3-2]]\n<<silently>>\n<<fadeinsound "In_the_House.mp3">>\n<<fadeoutsound "Walking_Dead_Theme_Song.mp3">>\n<<endsilently>>\n[[University]] Avenue will take you as far West as you need, and you can cut to Tripp along Babcock Drive quickly. Youll be going through the entire middle section of campus.\n \n[[Bascom Hill|Bascom]] rises up in front of you. Its a steep walk, but Bascom to Observatory is probably the most direct route. Youd be passing by fewer buildings, but its the heart of campus.\n \n[[Lakeshore Path|Lakeshore]] is creepy, isolated, and just the sort of place where youd get murdered in a horror movie. But on the other hand, its never very crowded, and there arent nearly as many buildings that you have to pass by.\n\n\n

In the Orchestra Room you find enough instruments to supply a whole high school band. Many are way too big to use, but theres a promising a violin that feels good in your hand and a set of cymbals.\n[img[Violin2]]\nThe [[violin]] seems effective, but is going to break pretty fast. Better not get into more than one fight on the way.\n[img[cymbal]]\nTwo cymbals seem little excessive. Youre going to want a free hand, so you decide to leave one of the [[cymbals|Cymbal]] behind.\n\n[[Find Something Else|Find Shaun]]

<<if $transportation eq "walk">>\nYou cautiously set off West down University Avenue, weaving through the wreckage of abandoned cars and garbage. You can hear groans coming from the buildings along the way, but theres no one in sight. The trip seems to go painstakingly slow, cautious as you are. Grainger crawls by to be replaced by a slowly passing Chemistry building. Youre sneaking across Charter when your phone goes off again, breaking the silence.\n\n<<timedinsert 10s>><<display 'WiscAlert2.5'>><<endtimedinsert>>\n\n<<timedinsert 15s>>Youre cut off from all sides.\n\n[[Time to take a stand.|Fight2]]<<endtimedinsert>>\n<<else>>\nYou waste no time ripping down University on your bike. Theres a lot of buildings that could have God knows what in them, and you dont mean to find out. Its tricky going, avoiding all the cars and debris, but you do your best to avoid slowing down. Youre just crossing Charter when your phone goes off again, the only other sound beyond the clinking of your bike chain. \n \n<<timedinsert 8s>>Theres a brief moment of silence after your phone goes off. Then you hear a guttural groan in the distance, followed by another. Looks like youve drawn some attention. As the crescendo grows, you can see zombies pouring out of the buildings around you. A pack is running down the Charter Hill, coming straight for you. The doors of Chamberlin are a seething mass of zombies, trying to get through the doors. Even more are pouring out of Chemistry and Psychology, headed at you in haggard run. From the wreckage of abandoned cars on University, another pack emerges.<<endtimedinsert>>\n \n<<timedinsert 14s>>Everything gets a bit dodgy for a couple minutes, but with a lot of luck and some expert maneuvering, you find yourself biking away from the entire horde unscathed. Good thing you grabbed a bike; the zombies couldnt keep up. Another couple minutes of biking, and you safely arrive at [[Tripp Circle]].<<endtimedinsert>>\n<<endif>>\n
You waste no time getting to Shaun's room. You quietly knock on his door and whisper "It's me." The door whips open and you find yourself pulled into the room before you can even register what just happened. Shaun double locks the door and barricades it with his dresser before turning to give you a hug. You see he has a handgun pistol, probably because his dad is a police officer.\n\n<<timedinsert 6s>>Shaun: "You fucker! I knew you'd make it over here! What took you so long?"<<endtimedinsert>>\n<<timedinsert 8s>>You: "Yeah, I ran into a couple of zombies along the way. You're the one with the gun. Why didn't you come get me?"<<endtimedinsert>>\n\n<<timedinsert 12s>>For the first time today, you find yourself smiling. You feel safe. Just as you relax with your best friend, your phone rings one last time. You cant help but wonder why you havent turned it off by now.<<endtimedinsert>>\n\n<<timedgoto "WiscAlert4" 23s>>

[[Go to bathroom and shower|Shower]] or [[Just rush to class |Walking out to the first class]] to get a good seat in Comm Arts 200: Introduction to Digital Communication. \n\n\n
<<if $transportation eq "walk">> \nYou cut up Park Street to the lake, then turn West to head down Lakeshore Path. The path is pretty muddy from yesterday's rainstorm, but blessedly devoid of people and zombies. Walking amidst all the trees, with the lake to your right, its easy to forget how messed up the world has gotten today. You exit to street level and begin to pick up on the not-so-subtle carnage that has ravaged Madison this morning. Tipped over trash cans, abandoned cars and bikes, backpacks and garbage littering the streets. Even the bike racks have been upended.\n \n<<timedinsert 3s>>Nerves a little jittery still, you walk over to the campus map posted on the street corner.
